<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-synchronizer-sequencer-abstractsequencerpruningstatus"></a>

### `AbstractSequencerPruningStatus`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/AbstractSequencerPruningStatus.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait AbstractSequencerPruningStatus extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

Using the member details, calculate based on their acknowledgements when is the latest point we can safely prune without losing any data that may still be read.

abstract class BaseSequencer extends Sequencer with NamedLogging with Spanning

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-synchronizer-sequencer-conflictingpayloadidexception"></a>

### `ConflictingPayloadIdException`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/ConflictingPayloadIdException.html)

**Signature**

```text
final class ConflictingPayloadIdException extends SequencerWriterException
```

**Summary**

We intentionally use an unsafe storage method for writing payloads to take advantage of a full connection pool for performance. However this means if a HA Sequencer Writer has lost its instance lock it may still attempt to write payloads while another Sequencer Writer is active with the same instance index. As we use this instance index to generate an (almost) conflict free payload id, in this circumstance there is a slim chance that we may attempt to write conflicting payloads with the same id. If we were using a simple idempotent write approach this could result in the active sequencer writing an event with a payload from the offline writer process (and not the payload it is expecting). This would be a terrible and difficult to diagnose corruption issue.

**Members**

No members found for this type in the configured artifacts.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-synchronizer-sequencer-directsequencerclienttransport"></a>

### `DirectSequencerClientTransport`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/DirectSequencerClientTransport.html)

**Signature**

```text
class DirectSequencerClientTransport extends SequencerClientTransport with SequencerClientTransportPekko with NamedLogging
```

**Summary**

This transport is meant to be used to create a sequencer client that connects directly to an in-process sequencer. Needed for cases when the sequencer node itself needs to listen to specific events such as identity events.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-synchronizer-sequencer-directsequencerconnectionxpool"></a>

### `DirectSequencerConnectionXPool`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/DirectSequencerConnectionXPool.html)

**Signature**

```text
class DirectSequencerConnectionXPool extends SequencerConnectionXPool
```

**Summary**

This connection pool is meant to be used to create a sequencer client that connects directly to an in-process sequencer. Needed for cases when the sequencer node itself needs to listen to specific events such as identity events.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-synchronizer-sequencer-pollingeventsignaller"></a>

### `PollingEventSignaller`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/PollingEventSignaller.html)

**Signature**

```text
class PollingEventSignaller extends EventSignaller with NamedLogging
```

**Summary**

Ignore local writes and simply trigger reads periodically based on a static polling interval. Suitable for horizontally scaled sequencers where the local process will not have in-process visibility of all writes.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-synchronizer-sequencer-progresssupervisor"></a>

### `ProgressSupervisor`

- Introduced: `3.4.11`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/ProgressSupervisor.html)

**Signature**

```text
class ProgressSupervisor extends NamedLogging
```

**Summary**

ProgressSupervisor is a component that is meant to monitor anomalies in the node's operation, (i.e. node not making progressing), not covered by the conventional health checks, based on timing and expectations of processing progress of a data flow. It is meant to trigger alerts and possibly remedial actions:

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-synchronizer-sequencer-sequencedwrite"></a>

### `SequencedWrite`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/SequencedWrite.html)

**Signature**

```text
sealed trait SequencedWrite extends HasTraceContext
```

**Summary**

A write that we've assigned a timestamp to. We drag these over the same clock so we can ensure earlier items have lower timestamps and later items have higher timestamps. This is very helpful, essential you may say, for correctly setting the watermark while ensuring an event with an earlier timestamp will not be written.

- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/SequencerOfflineException.html)

**Signature**

```text
final class SequencerOfflineException extends SequencerWriterException
```

**Summary**

Throw as an error in the pekko stream when we discover that our currently running sequencer writer has been marked as offline.

No members found for this type in the configured artifacts.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-synchronizer-sequencer-sequencerwriter"></a>

### `SequencerWriter`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/SequencerWriter.html)

**Signature**

```text
class SequencerWriter extends NamedLogging with FlagCloseableAsync with HasCloseContext
```

**Summary**

The Writer component is in practice a little state machine that will run crash recovery on startup then create a running SequencerWriterSource. If this materialized Sequencer flow then crashes with an exception that can be recovered by running crash recovery it will then go through this process and attempt to restart the flow.

**Signature**

```text
trait SequencerWriterStoreFactory extends AutoCloseable
```

**Summary**

Create instances for a sequencer.store.SequencerWriterStore and a predicate to know whether we can recreate a sequencer writer on failures encountered potentially during storage. Implements AutoClosable so implementations can use lifecycle.FlagCloseable to short circuit retry attempts.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-synchronizer-sequencer-writepayloadsflow"></a>

### `WritePayloadsFlow`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/WritePayloadsFlow$.html)

**Signature**

```text
object WritePayloadsFlow
```

**Summary**

Extract the payloads of events and write them in batches to the payloads table. As order does not matter at this point allow writing batches concurrently up to the concurrency specified by SequencerWriterConfig.payloadWriteMaxConcurrency. Pass on the events with the payloads dropped and replaced by their payload ids.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-synchronizer-sequencer-writerstartuperror"></a>

### `WriterStartupError`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/WriterStartupError.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait WriterStartupError extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

Errors that can occur while starting the SequencerWriter. In the HA Sequencer Writer it is possible due to racy assignment of writer locks that the startup may fail. This is by design and starting the writer can simply be retried. However other errors such as discovering incorrect configuration or a unexpected commit mode will not be recoverable and the writer should propagate the failure.

**Members**

| Docs | Member | Introduced | Deprecated | Removed |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/WriterStartupError$.html#AllInstanceIndexesInUseextendsWriterStartupErrorwithProductwithSerializable) | `AllInstanceIndexesInUse` | `3.4.10` | - | - |
